<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bfc6db28-52e1-4833-9c78-ff82ad804e66'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer8611073316278449646"><i>See me just as I see you . . .</i><br/><br/>Colin Hancock is giving his second chance his best shot. With a history of violence and bad decisions behind him and the threat of prison dogging his every step, he's determined to walk a straight line. To Colin, that means applying himself single-mindedly toward his teaching degree and avoiding everything that proved destructive in his earlie</span>
  <span id="freeText8611073316278449646" style="display:none"><i>See me just as I see you . . .</i><br /><br />Colin Hancock is giving his second chance his best shot. With a history of violence and bad decisions behind him and the threat of prison dogging his every step, he's determined to walk a straight line. To Colin, that means applying himself single-mindedly toward his teaching degree and avoiding everything that proved destructive in his earlier life. Reminding himself daily of his hard-earned lessons, the last thing he is looking for is a serious relationship.<br /><br />Maria Sanchez, the hardworking daughter of Mexican immigrants, is the picture of conventional success. With a degree from Duke Law School and a job at a prestigious firm in Wilmington, she is a dark-haired beauty with a seemingly flawless professional track record. And yet Maria has a traumatic history of her own, one that compelled her to return to her hometown and left her questioning so much of what she once believed.<br /><br />A chance encounter on a rain-swept road will alter the course of both Colin and Maria's lives, challenging deeply held assumptions about each other and ultimately, themselves. As love unexpectedly takes hold between them, they dare to envision what a future together could possibly look like . . . until menacing reminders of events in Maria's past begin to surface.<br /><br />Rich in emotion and fueled with suspense, SEE ME reminds us that love is sometimes forged in the crises that threaten to shatter us . . . and that those who see us for who we truly are may not always be the ones easiest to recognize.<b>
  <br />
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8611073316278449646" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1431967997" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12943468236970791136"><b>2.5 Stars</b><p>"Okay".........something's missing here........When I decide to read a Nicholas Sparks novel, I pretty much know and look forward to what I'm going to get, but <b>SEE ME</b> just did not work. It had a somewhat different flair <i>(which is "Okay")</i> with a stalker on the loose and an unlikely leading man with a dark history and hot temper added to the "mediocre" romantic mix, but..........</p><p>I'm sorry to say, <b>SEE ME</b> has turned out to be my least favorite NS read. The love connection lacked real feelin</p></span>
  <span id="freeText12943468236970791136" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars</b><p>"Okay".........something's missing here........When I decide to read a Nicholas Sparks novel, I pretty much know and look forward to what I'm going to get, but <b>SEE ME</b> just did not work. It had a somewhat different flair <i>(which is "Okay")</i> with a stalker on the loose and an unlikely leading man with a dark history and hot temper added to the "mediocre" romantic mix, but..........</p><p>I'm sorry to say, <b>SEE ME</b> has turned out to be my least favorite NS read. The love connection lacked real feeling, the characters were ho hum, and the prose tedious and a bit erratic with <u>way</u> too many "Okay's".</p><p>Overall, an "Okay" read that was definitely missing the <b>"spark".</b></p></span>

<div id="review_1237262314" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1237262314" />
    <a title="Krystal Bond" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9299051-krystal-bond"><img alt="Krystal Bond" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573444260p2/9299051.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1237262314?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Krystal Bond" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Krystal Bond" href="/user/show/9299051-krystal-bond">Krystal Bond</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1237262314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18211874417908920160">Nicholas Sparks does it once again. Yet another well written story about love, with a bit of mystery and suspense thrown into the mix. The story was a bit slow going at first, I believe this is his longest novel yet. It almost felt a bit to descriptive to start off, but when I got a little over halfway through I could hardly put it down. It ended up being just as lovely and thrilling as most all of his stories. I'll be shocked if I ever dislike one of his novels. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1330755314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7984239829027556163"><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445619036ra/16682162.gif' width='290' height='45' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>OK, where to start...<br/><b>I LOVED IT!</b><br/>I've read all Nicholas Sparks books so far and I loved them all - and I think I cried A LOT with every book. Unlike most of my reading-blogging-friends, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/41865.Twilight__Twilight___1_' title='Twilight (Twilight, #1) by Stephenie Meyer' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twilight</a> did NOT start my reading-addiction - it was <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3473.A_Walk_to_Remember' title='A Walk to Remember by Nicholas Sparks' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Walk to Remember</a> ♥<br/><br/>This time....hm....<br/>I cried a tiny little bit - I knew where the story was going from pretty much the very first time the bad guy was mentioned - the story was a bit slow, too long, too uneventful in the beginning - <b>BUT</b> ... it was refreshingl</span>
  <span id="freeText7984239829027556163" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445619036ra/16682162.gif" width="290" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>OK, where to start...<br><b>I LOVED IT!</b><br>I've read all Nicholas Sparks books so far and I loved them all - and I think I cried A LOT with every book. Unlike most of my reading-blogging-friends, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/41865.Twilight__Twilight___1_" title="Twilight (Twilight, #1) by Stephenie Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Twilight</a> did NOT start my reading-addiction - it was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3473.A_Walk_to_Remember" title="A Walk to Remember by Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">A Walk to Remember</a> ♥<br><br>This time....hm....<br>I cried a tiny little bit - I knew where the story was going from pretty much the very first time the bad guy was mentioned - the story was a bit slow, too long, too uneventful in the beginning - <b>BUT</b> ... it was refreshingly non-sparksy-interesting.<br><br>I don't know if it was because it's his first published book post-divorce, but I really enjoyed the freshness of it.<br><br>It wasn't Nicholas-Sparks-Cheesy at all. If I hadn't known it was Nicholas Sparks, I would've thought it was a nice New Adult Romantic Suspense written by a woman.<br><br>I loved Colin. He was such a non-Nicholas-Sparks guy.<br>And I looooved his OKAYs! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445619036ra/16682163.gif" width="370" height="52" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What an amazing thing to come up with for a character.<br>Well, I guess there's a person somewhere in Nicholas's life, who does that okay-thing, but still, I loved it!<br>I would be totally on-the-verge-of-killing-him-frustrated if someone in my life talked like that though. ☺<br><br>If you expect a cry-nonstop-cheesy-romance thingy - don't! It's different this time, like his old romances, with the suspense parts. I really liked it. Could've used an editor with a better cutting-device - it was a tiny bit too long. ☺<br><br><b>READ IT - make up your own mind about it - don't mind me ☺</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432568184i/14982632.png" width="370" height="143" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442943030i/16296666.png" width="370" height="58" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://amzn.to/1LrFH5Z" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1419242210" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1419242210" />
    <a title="Emily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12717867-emily"><img alt="Emily" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1419242210?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/12717867-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1419242210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15471418375755851468">If you're wondering if Nicholas Sparks still has it after his divorce, he doesn't. <br/><br/>This was not what I expected. It was not a love story. It was a stalker, suspense, twist and turn story. With so much detail oh my lord over the top details! <br/><br/>Maybe other people will like it but I was so disappointed. I didn't even cry!!!!! I just wanted it to be over. And I skimmed so much. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1416376210" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1416376210" />
    <a title="Debbie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20335081-debbie"><img alt="Debbie" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1416376210?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debbie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debbie" href="/user/show/20335081-debbie">Debbie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25881836-see-me">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1416376210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13643769750479316843">Disappointed. I am a huge fan of Nicholas Sparks, but this book just didn't live up to the hype. I guessed at almost all of the plot twists before they happened, so there were no real surprises. I know this book was a step into a new genre for him, but I hope he goes back to writing what he does best. If the book had been written by anyone other than Nicholas Sparks, I would have put it down halfway through and not even finished it. Just ... Disappointed ...</span>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45911840-alice-married-to-books?shelf=alice-reads-adult-fiction">alice-reads-adult-fiction</a>,

<span id="freeTextContainer16379978101634317562">The last 100 pages of this book just destroyed me, no joke. It was an edge on your seat type thrill that I couldn't put the book down without having to see it through to the end. If you know me well, you will know that I actually do enjoy reading books by Nicholas Sparks and See Me was a good read. The plot followed Colin, a 28 year old having a second chance in life by training to be a teacher in College after he became aggressive, ended up on the wrong side of the law and having his parents th</span>
  <span id="freeText16379978101634317562" style="display:none">The last 100 pages of this book just destroyed me, no joke. It was an edge on your seat type thrill that I couldn't put the book down without having to see it through to the end. If you know me well, you will know that I actually do enjoy reading books by Nicholas Sparks and See Me was a good read. The plot followed Colin, a 28 year old having a second chance in life by training to be a teacher in College after he became aggressive, ended up on the wrong side of the law and having his parents throw him out. The other main character Maria is also 28 and works as a lawyer having a sister Serena always looking out for her. When Colin and Maria's paths cross due to a car tyre, so does the start of a potential blossoming romance. However, Maria has some secrets of her own and once it becomes clear the two of them are an item, strange things start happening to her such as anonymous notes. The thing is, this has happened to her before and they were the result of a case in which a young girl was stalked and murdered.<br /><br />The story itself is just under 500 pages long and does have a lot of backstory so be prepared to hear lots of things about both main characters past as well as their present occupations. The part of Colin being a MMA fighter also interested me since I hadn't read a story before in which the main character did MMA. It was a good read, just a little bit long but be prepared for the ending because I definitely did not see it coming.<br /><br />Final star rating: 3.5 out of 5 stars!<br /><br />I borrowed a copy of this from my local library.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dale Harcombe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dale Harcombe" href="/user/show/4800708-dale-harcombe">Dale Harcombe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1365804772" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18238501291305219330">This novel starts off with an unidentified male person wanting vengeance on Maria Sanchez. It then introduces the two main characters. Colin Hancock, who has in the past had a chequered history with the law. He is now seeking to change his life, earn a teaching degree and have his criminal record expunged. One rainy night he meets Maria Sanchez, who is a lawyer. From then on chapters are told alternately between Colin and Maria. The novel turns into a love story, which is no surprise given that </span>
  <span id="freeText18238501291305219330" style="display:none">This novel starts off with an unidentified male person wanting vengeance on Maria Sanchez. It then introduces the two main characters. Colin Hancock, who has in the past had a chequered history with the law. He is now seeking to change his life, earn a teaching degree and have his criminal record expunged. One rainy night he meets Maria Sanchez, who is a lawyer. From then on chapters are told alternately between Colin and Maria. The novel turns into a love story, which is no surprise given that the author is Nicholas Sparks. But the threat of vengeance from that first chapter still hovers. Eventually it escalates to being more than just a threat. But who is the person seeking vengeance?<br />I enjoyed this novel and kept wanting to read it at every opportunity. I really liked some of the minor characters in the novel, like Lily, fiancée of Colin’s friend Evan and Serena, Maria’s sister. I also liked Colin’s honesty and the way he responded to questions, even if it wasn’t always the answer people wanted to hear. There is a lot of dialogue in this novel and I enjoyed some of the conversations that ensued.<br />I admit to being a fan of Nicholas Sparks and the rate I read this shows how I enjoyed it, even if I had figured out who was responsible for the stalking of Maria. If you are a Nicholas Sparks’ fan you should enjoy it. It is more than just a love story. In fact, the romance tends to almost take second place to the vengeance and thriller aspects. This is another one I can see being made into a movie.<br /></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText6456297536382010530" style="display:none">3.5 Stars<br /><br />Colin was the third child and only child of his parents. His parents sent him to a military school where did wrestling, boxing and judo. He was a violent and angry man with no plans for his life until he decided to go to college at the age of 25. Evan his friend was an accountant and financial planner. Colin over in Evan's apartment on rent. <br /><br />Maria was a lawyer who worked at the district attorney's office. She and Colin met on the highway when her car broke and Colin helped her with it. Maria was having a hard time because of her one colleague. Maria's sister Serena and Colin studied in the same class, so she took her to the bar where he worked. Together they spent some time and told one another stories from their pasts and agreed to meet next on Sunday for paddle boarding. Eventually they started liking one another. <br /><br />One day Maria received a bouquet at her office and thought Colin might have sent it, but he didn't send any. That day onwards things started to change as Maria kept getting weird cards, drinks for free, etc., all from an unknown person. It turned that someone from a previous case which didn't work out was after her life and wanted to inflict the same pain on Maria and her family that he had to face. <br /><br />Maria resigned from her job and joined a startup firm with Jill. Colin and Evan tracked down the attacker after much struggle. They saved Serena who was kidnapped. <br /><br />This novel will keep you on your nerves. <span id="freeTextContainer5936702857426008025">I've loved everything Nicholas Sparks has ever written...until now.<br/><br/>I preordered this book and counted down the days until its release. It automatically downloaded on my Kindle and I began reading. I read the prologue and exited the book, assuming I had somehow started to read the wrong thing. No, it was See Me. I read the first chapter and googled the book to make sure it hadn't been written by someone with a similar name. No, it was the same Nicholas Sparks who wrote The Notebook and At First S</span>
  <span id="freeText5936702857426008025" style="display:none">I've loved everything Nicholas Sparks has ever written...until now.<br /><br />I preordered this book and counted down the days until its release. It automatically downloaded on my Kindle and I began reading. I read the prologue and exited the book, assuming I had somehow started to read the wrong thing. No, it was See Me. I read the first chapter and googled the book to make sure it hadn't been written by someone with a similar name. No, it was the same Nicholas Sparks who wrote The Notebook and At First Sight. So I pressed on and finished the entire thing, hoping he would somehow work his romantic literary magic. It never happened. This book was 77% dialogue and 98% of that was poorly written. WHO TALKS LIKE THIS? No one, that's who.<br /><br />This is the first Nicholas Sparks novel where I haven't fallen in love along with the characters. And the thing is, if it had by written by someone else, it's not a terrible book. It's just lacking everything I love about Nicholas Sparks. Such a disappointment.</span>

<div id="review_1973461937" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1973461937" />
    <a title="Sylvie {on semi-hiatus}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/64899539-sylvie-on-semi-hiatus"><img alt="Sylvie {on semi-hiatus}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534779997p2/64899539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1973461937?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sylvie {on semi-hiatus}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sylvie {on semi-hiatus}" href="/user/show/64899539-sylvie-on-semi-hiatus">Sylvie {on semi-hiatus}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/64899539-sylvie-on-semi-hiatus?shelf=nicholas-sparks">nicholas-sparks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/64899539-sylvie-on-semi-hiatus?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/64899539-sylvie-on-semi-hiatus?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1973461937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16378541397491619304">3.5 stars<br/><br/>It was as if Nicholas Sparks meets Stephen King, but in milder way, since Stephen's books are much more darker and suspenseful. Yet again that's just typical of the author since there are always blossoms an immediate chemistry and attraction with Spark's main characters. Nevertheless, I didn't like how he changed his usual style in this book, he always focuses more on the romance and the main characters' developing relationship, the concept of this novel leaned more on the suspense. Col</span>
  <span id="freeText16378541397491619304" style="display:none">3.5 stars<br /><br />It was as if Nicholas Sparks meets Stephen King, but in milder way, since Stephen's books are much more darker and suspenseful. Yet again that's just typical of the author since there are always blossoms an immediate chemistry and attraction with Spark's main characters. Nevertheless, I didn't like how he changed his usual style in this book, he always focuses more on the romance and the main characters' developing relationship, the concept of this novel leaned more on the suspense. Collin and Maria's first meet wasn’t love at first sight but it was definitely attraction at first sight, altough their relationship progressed very quickly. The way Nicholas describes romantic moments in his books is astonishing, it sweeps you off your feet, but admittedly it didn't happen to be great in this book.<br /><br />There was a major stalker situation going on in this book, however it was interesting but in the mean time gave me a headache. I kept suspecting on 5 different people at the same time, the author sure kept me of the edge of my seat even in the epilogue. The characters were well written, especially the side characters (Colin and Maria's friends to be more particular). What was missing in the book in my opinion was that Collin never contacted neither his parents nor to his sisters, I understand why he was keeping his distance from his parents because they've been keeping up with his failiures and mess for a really long time but eventualy gave up on him, due to his immaturity and for being irresponsible. Despite Collin being a troubled young man at an early age he turned out amazing, caring and passionate man. And yet the whole thing was a cliche. Why? Because Maria is a good girl and Collin is a bad boy but they never let their reputation or pasts get into their relationship, I wasn't really a fan of their love story, I'm not saying it was bad but it was nothing near good comparing to his other novels like: The Notebook or The Longest Ride.<br /><br />Great narrative in the vein of his other books, however the pace was a bit slow. <br /><br />I wouldn't describe this book as a total utter disappointement, but it didn't meet my expectations either.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16378541397491619304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_1385171166" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1385171166" />
    <a title="Judy D Collins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11063006-judy-d-collins"><img alt="Judy D Collins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577847504p2/11063006.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1385171166?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Judy D Collins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Judy D Collins" href="/user/show/11063006-judy-d-collins">Judy D Collins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=books-read-in-2015">books-read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=north-carolina">north-carolina</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=2015-new-releases">2015-new-releases</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=nicholas-sparks">nicholas-sparks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=relationships">relationships</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11063006-judy-d-collins?shelf=womens-fiction">womens-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1385171166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer953565822658449370">Gifted Southern storyteller, <i>Nicholas Sparks </i> continues to “pull out all the stops” with his new romantic thriller, <b>SEE ME </b> — <i>assured to be yet another bestseller, and blockbuster movie. </i><br/><br/><b>A novel </b> of second chances, as the past and present collide, with a roller-coaster ride of emotion, suspense, mystery, and thriller . . <i>And, as always, a love story running in the background, found in the most likely of places.</i><br/><br/><b>SEE ME, just as I see you </b>. . . <i>what powerful words.</i><br/><br/><b>Set in Wilmington, </b> North Carolina</span>
  <span id="freeText953565822658449370" style="display:none">Gifted Southern storyteller, <i>Nicholas Sparks </i> continues to “pull out all the stops” with his new romantic thriller, <b>SEE ME </b> — <i>assured to be yet another bestseller, and blockbuster movie. </i><br /><br /><b>A novel </b> of second chances, as the past and present collide, with a roller-coaster ride of emotion, suspense, mystery, and thriller . . <i>And, as always, a love story running in the background, found in the most likely of places.</i><br /><br /><b>SEE ME, just as I see you </b>. . . <i>what powerful words.</i><br /><br /><b>Set in Wilmington, </b> North Carolina – the iconic novelist has published eighteen novels and two non-fiction books. <b>SEE ME,</b> focuses on a young man named Colin Hancock, who is trying to shed negative influences in his life, and Maria Sanchez, a hardworking lawyer and daughter of Mexican immigrants who has her own dark past. The protagonists meet by chance, when she has car trouble during a rainstorm; however, their budding romance is threatened by a hidden menace.<br /><br /><b>You can depend </b> on two things: Sparks' books being set in NC and a couple will fall in love. Let me start out by saying, <b>SEE ME </b> offers more intrigue than some of his previous books. More of a twisty mystery thriller, keeping the reader in the dark, as to the identity of the bad guy. <br /><br /><b> Colin Hancock</b> has a history with an unfortunate past, prone to fights and violence. From PTSD, ADHD, a childhood of bullying, trouble with the law---and many wrong turns along the way. From a wealthy family raised by a series of nannies, from one fight to another with serious issues. His parents shipped him off to military school -a downward spiral. At twenty-five, he was given a second chance. <i> (You will love his famous "OK". His answer to everything is, "just, OK", showing no emotion). </i><br /><br /><b>Presently, Colin</b> is doing his best to stay on the straight and narrow. He is focused, and determined to achieve his goals. Back to college at UNC Wilmington, at age twenty-eight he is studying to be a teacher, to mentor children. With religious trips to the gym, and lots of anger management classes behind him, to control his demons, while working as a bartender in the local Wilmington area. He continues to be involved in MMA-Mixed Martial Arts as a means to keep his violence intact, with a perfect GPA. <br /><br />He continues to stay out of trouble, and does not put himself in or around any environment which could lead to fights, or screw up his parole. He has the looks, the ripped muscular body, to turn heads; however, a little rough around the edges with tattoos, a tough outward appearance. His personality is cut and dry, and is not about trying to impress or engage in conversation. His past crime record has been expunged (thanks to his dad); however, if he screws up one more time, he is back in prison. <i>There is a local cop just lurking, waiting for him to screw up again, so he can put him away. </i><br /><br /><b>Colin lives in a downstairs </b> apartment, he rents from his oldest best friend (landlord), conservative--Evan, an accountant, a financial planner, and his beautiful fiancée, Lilly who is around most of the time. His best friend has been there for him through thick and thin, and Lilly, the prim and proper society Charleston Southern Belle, is always there to offer her advice and “Bless your Heart” reassurance; a drop dead debutante, and an accent as sweet as honey. Lilly has tutored him in the evenings, and kept him from making impulsive decisions, as well as Evan helping to keep him in line. He has his work, MMA, and his studies. He knows his limits and keeps his anger in check. <br /><br /><b>Maria, age twenty-eight, </b> believes in working hard to achieve your status and career goals. The daughter of Mexican immigrants, she comes from a very close knit family. She has beauty, charm, and brains. Her parents and family, own and operate a local Mexican restaurant. She and her beautiful sister (she is funny), and her best friend. The two sisters attend weekly brunches with family—they like to keep their personal lives private, from their parents conservative eyes. <br /> <br /><b>With a law degree</b> from Duke University, Hispanic Maria is now trying to fit in with a prestigious law firm in Wilmington, NC, and desires to make partner. She left a DA position in Charlotte, NC, after a horrific case she was involved in with one of her clients, which led to her death. The case still haunts her, along with the stress of her job, as why the decision to move to Wilmington. However, there is an older married partner of the firm, sexually harassing the women, and putting the pressure on her. She wants no part of this. In the meantime, her sister is always after her about dating. She is not interested, and has enough pressure at work-She has no time for a personal life. <br /><br /><b>When Maria gets stuck </b> on the side of the road in the middle of nowhere, with a flat tire--Colin steps out of his Camaro stopping by to offer his assistance--she is afraid of him. He is scary looking, after a fight the previous night (he fights competitively), he is a fright. All she needs is a scary escaped convict. She does not need his help. She cannot find her phone and is frantic, now late for an important appointment. They wind up meeting again later. Her younger sister happens to be in class with Colin, and when they later go out for drinks at the bar where he works, their paths cross once again.<br /><br /><b>An unexpected connection. </b> They wind up meeting again, slowly become friends and openly share their past. They struggle trying to deal with their mismatched backgrounds. However, when meeting the parents, does not go so well, with Colin’s violent past. With numerous obstacles trying to pull them apart, can they possibly have a future together?<br /><br /><b>There is something bigger</b> going on---an evil plan, playing out in the background, involving a past event. Vengeance. A dangerous stalker, and Maria’s family is targeted. From Serena, Maria’s sister, to Maria . . . someone knows their every move. This is where the danger and mystery comes front and center in the story. <br /><br /><b>When a past case </b> of revenge begins to cause danger for Maria’s family, Colin will risk it all to save the woman he loves. Crossing many genres, this is not a sappy love story; it is part psychological, crime, mystery, and thriller. Layers of suspense, surrounding a love story with characters from different walks of life. <br /><br /><b>SEE ME </b> offers a different twist, keeping readers on their toes, turning pages, by keeping the nature of the threat obscured. Until the end, you do not know the identity of the hidden bad guy.<br /><br /><i>What can you say about Nicholas Sparks that has not been said? </i> One of the top authors of this genre- mastering romantic suspense. Each of his books dive deep into human emotions and dynamics, with layers of tragedy and loss, with well-developed everyday characters, seeking second chances when unfortunate elements continue to pull them down. <i>In the end, they come out stronger. </i><br /><br />Since I have read all his books, and movies, everyone asks how SEE ME compares? Each book is unique and delivers a different story and set of circumstances. What I enjoy about his work, is each book delivers a different emotion---some have more mystery, crime, or suspense, than others. There is always strong powers of conflict. <br /><br /><b>SEE ME is powerful;</b> however, did not find myself with endless tears; not quite as dramatic as some in the past; however, more of a character-driven novel, and this is where it shines. Sparks does a fantastic job of combining love story with thriller components, as he allows the love story to take more of a back seat, to the danger in the forefront. <br /><br />As a Charlotte, NC native, raising my family in Winston-Salem, NC and having worked in Charleston, SC---it is always nice to hear mentions of familiar places in the NC/SC area. All you <i>Dorothea Benton Frank and Mary Kay Andrews’ fans </i> will enjoy the humor of Lilly--as she mentors Colin --how to dance, and what clothes to wear, as she works to smooth out some of Colin’s rough edges to make him acceptable in the eyes of his new found relationship and her family. <br /><br />I always pre-order Sparks’ audiobooks when he has a new release. Over past years, his audiobooks have accompanied me with my long road trips from NC back to Florida, or NC to Georgia. <br /><br /><b>Audiobook: </b> The narrator, <i>Christopher Ryan Grant </i> one of the BEST!! He delivered an outstanding performance, ideal with a wide range of voices and personalities; for the quiet dry, Colin; Hispanic, Maria; the funny Serena; parents, the kick ass attorney, Jill; the all American boy, Evan; the Southern cop; and the “to die” for performance of Lilly, the Southern Belle. Highly recommend the audiobook, as Sparks and Grant, make for one stoppable team! <br /><br />My only negative: The front cover does not truly capture the mood of the story, as his previous books; however, sure with the upcoming formats and publications, it may change. <br /><br /><b>Upcoming Sparks News:</b> <i> If you haven't heard </i> The New Bern author is working with ABC to develop a comedy titled “The Next Chapter,” which centers on a best-selling romance novelist who is recently divorced. Ten of Sparks' novels have been turned into movies and he expects his new film production company, Nicholas Sparks Productions, will eventually adapt "See Me." "The Choice," which is scheduled to release in February, will be the company's first film and a script for "The Guardian" is in the works.<br /><br /><i>Can't wait to see what is next! </i><br /><br /><a href="http://www.judithdcollinsconsulting.com/#!See-Me/cmoa/55d0d5fa0cf2b503a1a58e9d" rel="nofollow noopener"> JDCMustReadBooks </a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="953565822658449370" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Then at least I'll have some vindication for how much of a true let down this was. Not only did I not like the characters and not like the main love story, it pissed me off. It was such an awful calculated "thriller" where the characters couldn't put the pieces together and made you cringe and yell at the book constantly for just how stupid they were. Why can't Sparks just stick to what he does best, a genuine honest </span>
  <span id="freeText12278115206230672138" style="display:none">I hope Nicholas Sparks hated writing this novel as much as I hated reading it. Then at least I'll have some vindication for how much of a true let down this was. Not only did I not like the characters and not like the main love story, it pissed me off. It was such an awful calculated "thriller" where the characters couldn't put the pieces together and made you cringe and yell at the book constantly for just how stupid they were. Why can't Sparks just stick to what he does best, a genuine honest love story? I'm just flummoxed this even got published.</span>

<div id="review_1330309381" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1330309381" />
    <a title="Christina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14066678-christina"><img alt="Christina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481826762p2/14066678.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1330309381?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christina" href="/user/show/14066678-christina">Christina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1330309381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7741327721389000449">4 stars<br/><br/>While I usually tend to lean more towards YA books ( fantasy & dystopian being my faves ), I have a soft spot for Nicholas Sparks. I have read pretty much all his novels, own my favorites and watched all the ones that have been converted to movies. His books give me those warm, fuzzy feels that a girl needs every now and then. This being his newest one, it had a slightly darker feel than the others. <br/><br/>The book centers around Maria, a child of Mexican immigrants who became a lawyer and Colin</span>
  <span id="freeText7741327721389000449" style="display:none">4 stars<br /><br />While I usually tend to lean more towards YA books ( fantasy &amp; dystopian being my faves ), I have a soft spot for Nicholas Sparks. I have read pretty much all his novels, own my favorites and watched all the ones that have been converted to movies. His books give me those warm, fuzzy feels that a girl needs every now and then. This being his newest one, it had a slightly darker feel than the others. <br /><br />The book centers around Maria, a child of Mexican immigrants who became a lawyer and Colin, who has a troubled past and is trying to overcome that and become a school teacher. They cross paths one night in a chance meeting and slowly become a part of each other's lives. But Maria had some troubles of her own in the past, and those troubles start to catch up with her. <br /><br />I liked that very early on in the novel, you find out both Maria's and Colin's back stories. There's still a slight air of mystery throughout, but I still liked knowing the why of things and I liked being able to draw my own conclusions based on those stories and based on little details that emerge throughout the novel. I loved reading about the family dynamic with Maria and her sister, Serena and their parents. I liked how close knit they all were. But of course, my favorite part of pretty much any Nicholas Sparks novel is reading about the relationship and how it goes from attraction, to eventually love. Because, like most of his stories, this is first and foremost, a love story.<br /><br />Not my favorite novel by Sparks, but not a bad one by any means. It kept me guessing until the end and held my interest throughout, plus induced tears ( yes, Sparks tends to make me cry alot! ) not to mention had me loving Colin and rooting for him the whole time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7741327721389000449" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3647922830" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3647922830?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valérie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valérie" href="/user/show/67918882-val-rie">Valérie</a>
      </span>

          added it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3647922830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14662433094634845436">Maria, a busy lawyer, meets Colin, by a strange coincidence. The two couldn't be more different, but there is a spark between them. One day, Maria receives flowers and a highly questionable message that brings her past into the present. From that moment, the book is exclusively about that. The relationship between Maria and Colin is relegated to the background, which I personally find very sad. In my eyes, there are better Spark's books. With time, one doesn't want to read on. <br/><br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1308117097" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1308117097" />
    <a title="Kelsey Marie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9764479-kelsey-marie"><img alt="Kelsey Marie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595768113p2/9764479.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1308117097?book_show_action=true">Jun 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelsey Marie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelsey Marie" href="/user/show/9764479-kelsey-marie">Kelsey Marie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9764479-kelsey-marie?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9764479-kelsey-marie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1308117097" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9981054501045720380">*****For my full review of this brilliant book, stop by <a href='http://darlingandcompany.blogspot.com/2016/06/see-me-by-nicholas-sparks.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Darling & Co.</a>*****<br/><br/>So this book has been sitting on my TBR shelf for a while. Last October when it was published, I purchased the audiobook of it and then never listened to it. My thought process was that I would buy a book that was kind of long and then listen to it while I worked out; that didn't happen, and the book went unread/un-listened to. So this last weekend, I was sitting around reading different things, and I saw it sitting in my </span>
  <span id="freeText9981054501045720380" style="display:none">*****For my full review of this brilliant book, stop by <a href="http://darlingandcompany.blogspot.com/2016/06/see-me-by-nicholas-sparks.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Darling &amp; Co.</a>*****<br /><br />So this book has been sitting on my TBR shelf for a while. Last October when it was published, I purchased the audiobook of it and then never listened to it. My thought process was that I would buy a book that was kind of long and then listen to it while I worked out; that didn't happen, and the book went unread/un-listened to. So this last weekend, I was sitting around reading different things, and I saw it sitting in my Audible account and decided I would buy the actual book and maybe I would actually read it. And that is exactly what happened. I started listening to it at work yesterday and when I got home, I picked up the book and kept reading until the very last page. I don't know why I waited so long to read it because yesterday, I could not put it down, and I am still reeling with excitement on how wonderful the book is.<br /><br />This is only my second <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks" title="Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">Nicholas Sparks</a> novel, my first being <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15931.The_Notebook__The_Notebook___1_" title="The Notebook (The Notebook, #1) by Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">The Notebook</a> which I read after I saw the movie. I have seen multiple movies based off of his books, and for me, Nicholas Sparks is synonyms with tear jerker, bawling my eyes out for days on end, my heart being ripped out and shred into three million pieces. So needless to say, that's what I was expecting with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24820165.See_Me" title="See Me by Nicholas Sparks" rel="nofollow noopener">See Me</a>. I did not shed a single tear with this book, but not because I'm heartless, but because this book is suspenseful; it's like a mystery and a romance and so many things. There are so many layers to this novel, it's just brilliant! I really loved that it wasn't pure romance because I thought that's what I wanted, but it really wasn't. I wanted this. <br /><br />This book held so many surprises and was so wonderfully written. I feel so lucky that I have read so many brilliant books lately. My LOVE shelf is quickly filling up with more and more books!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9981054501045720380" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14031289666583791225"><br/>This is a very different Nicholas Sparks book! If you loved The Notebook or The Best of Me, See Me may not be for you. When I began reading See Me, I was disappointed in the story. Nicholas Sparks' new style was interesting but not great for me. The love connection between Colin and Maria lacked real feeling and appeared unlikely. See Me is definitely my least favourite NS read but it kept me engaged until the last chapter. 3 stars</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1652125351" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1652125351" />
    <a title="Mary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34699629-mary"><img alt="Mary" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1652125351?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary" href="/user/show/34699629-mary">Mary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1652125351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18131122958572646168">Ugh. Worst book from Nicholas Sparks ever. And worst book I've read in some time. I've been a fan of Nicholas Sparks for his previous works but there were so many places this went wrong.. <br/><br/>First, the characters: Maria, supposedly a smart, driven lawyer but portrayed as weak and insipid; Colin, an annoying combination of testosterone/rage and sensitive devotion to Maria; Evan and Lilly, a couple whose relationship is mainly her manipulating him with skimpy clothing and innuendos of sexual rewards </span>
  <span id="freeText18131122958572646168" style="display:none">Ugh. Worst book from Nicholas Sparks ever. And worst book I've read in some time. I've been a fan of Nicholas Sparks for his previous works but there were so many places this went wrong.. <br /><br />First, the characters: Maria, supposedly a smart, driven lawyer but portrayed as weak and insipid; Colin, an annoying combination of testosterone/rage and sensitive devotion to Maria; Evan and Lilly, a couple whose relationship is mainly her manipulating him with skimpy clothing and innuendos of sexual rewards for doing what she wanted and he, in turn, behaving like a puppy dog. <br /><br />Second, the dialogue, especially Colin's. No one talks like that, especially a testosterone-laden man.<br /><br />Third, the detailed descriptions. At times, I literally said aloud, "enough already, we get it!". This was likely exacerbated by the fact that I was listening to this as an audiobook and couldn't skim past the protracted and extraneous narratives. <br /><br />Finally, the plot line. I realize this is fiction but this is so far from plausible that instead of being a romantic thriller, it was merely irritating. The combination of over the top characters and contrived situations made it hard to enjoy the story. <br /><br />On his website, Nicholas Sparks says "I have to be honest with you: it is always a challenge for me to conceive a unique, compelling and original storyline; after eighteen novels, it’s even more difficult. When I wrote See Me, my singular goal was to surprise and delight readers." Sorry, Nicholas, you did not achieve your goal with me this time. Frankly, it seemed you were just trying too hard to churn out #18.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18131122958572646168" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1418761309" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1418761309" />
    <a title="☕️Kimberly  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5082615-kimberly"><img alt="☕️Kimberly  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577559843p2/5082615.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1418761309?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☕️Kimberly  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="☕️Kimberly  " href="/user/show/5082615-kimberly">☕️Kimberly  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781478955450" href="/book/show/25862103-see-me">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1418761309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8817756886629329174">See Me is a departure from the tear-inducing novels that Sparks typically writes and I appreciated the mystery, thriller and suspense angles. While I pieced together things, thanks to some carefully placed clues I nonetheless enjoyed both the characters and the twists.<br/><br/>A chance encounter has Colin Hancock and Maria Sánchez meeting and thanks to the help of another character, these two meet yet again and begin a friendship that quickly moves to romance. These two are opposites, and I loved the slo</span>
  <span id="freeText8817756886629329174" style="display:none">See Me is a departure from the tear-inducing novels that Sparks typically writes and I appreciated the mystery, thriller and suspense angles. While I pieced together things, thanks to some carefully placed clues I nonetheless enjoyed both the characters and the twists.<br /><br />A chance encounter has Colin Hancock and Maria Sánchez meeting and thanks to the help of another character, these two meet yet again and begin a friendship that quickly moves to romance. These two are opposites, and I loved the slow-paced romance.<br /><br />Colin Hancock is not your typical bad boy. He has anger issues and has made some sad choices in the past. However, when we meet Colin he is well on his way to improving himself. He is impulsive and flawed and while I did not agree with everything Colin did, I held to the fact that his intentions are honorable. Thankfully, we see growth in this quiet, damaged hero. Colin is the type of character you will either like or struggle to find a connection to. Having a sensitive son who speaks few words, made it easy for me to identify with Colin, although I abhorred his violent nature.<br /><br />Marie Sánchez recently suffered some trauma when a victim’s brother blamed her when the murderer was set free. She has recently moved back to her hometown and is lonely and deeply dissatisfied with her current employment situation. Maria was a bit of a contradiction at times. She is intelligent, educated and unwilling to settle, but sometimes she annoyed me with her behavior.Thankfully she was strong when it came to Colin and refused to short change herself.<br /><br />Secondary characters included friends, family and the law. They all added an interesting mix to the story. Friends and family grounded the characters and created normalcy against the suspenseful plot. A detective who hounds Colin provided tension. I worried he would royally screw up his chances. Questions of mental stability made our villain scary and unpredictable. Subtle threads of prejudice and preconceived conceptions were weaved throughout and gave the reader food for thought in a natural showing not telling way.<br /><br />The romance while present was secondary to the intense action. I loved the slow-build but felt it got a little lost in the middle. Their connection felt realistic and I appreciated that they found growth from within because of their interaction.<br /><br />Plot twists, action scenes and near death experiences ramped up the tension as the story progressed. Sparks added red herrings and clues along the way. For me the clues revealed things to quickly and made the tale predictable.<br /><br />Christopher Ryan’s narration of Colin felt spot on and he handled the female voices equally well. His pacing was well done and I didn't feel the urge to speed up the audio.<br /><br /><a href="http://caffeinatedbookreviewer.com/2015/12/see-me-by-nicholas-sparks.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> This review was originally posted on Caffeinated Book Reviewer</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8817756886629329174" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer44970491439191968">God damn you Nicholas Sparks!<br/><br/><i>See Me</i> WAS SO FREAKING GOOD! Then it ripped out my heart, stabbed it repeatedly, and then stomped on it a couple of times just for fun. Seriously, if I never read the last couple of chapters.. I would be completely fine. Yet here I am.. an emotional mess. GOD DAMMIT NICHOLAS!<br/><br/>This book followed Colin, a 28 year old, with a second chance in life training to be a teacher. Now I get teachers all the credit that they deserve.. it's not an easy job. It's also not one I wou</span>
  <span id="freeText44970491439191968" style="display:none">God damn you Nicholas Sparks!<br /><br /><i>See Me</i> WAS SO FREAKING GOOD! Then it ripped out my heart, stabbed it repeatedly, and then stomped on it a couple of times just for fun. Seriously, if I never read the last couple of chapters.. I would be completely fine. Yet here I am.. an emotional mess. GOD DAMMIT NICHOLAS!<br /><br />This book followed Colin, a 28 year old, with a second chance in life training to be a teacher. Now I get teachers all the credit that they deserve.. it's not an easy job. It's also not one I would have. I'm not a people person and if I get sass.. well I dish out back. Just not in a nice way. Long story short.. I'm a bitch and I'm a bigger bitch when someone constantly pushes my buttons.<br /><br />Back to this book. Colin meets Maria, who is a 28 year old lawyer, and there relationship/romance was soo good! I thrived on it! Then of course, Nicholas does his thing, and stuff starts happening. Maria has secrets that are sort of coming out.. like anonymous notes and shit. Then you find out there was murder and everything.. yeah shit hits the fan basically.<br /><br />I feel like this book was way too short.. mostly because I just miss the happiness of it all. Not the pages that basically broke my spirit. I'm so emotionally tired after this book.. I need more wine to cope with this. Or sleep.. maybe both.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1548640023" />
    <a title="Kristy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2705039-kristy"><img alt="Kristy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1453228324p2/2705039.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1548640023?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristy" href="/user/show/2705039-kristy">Kristy</a>

  <span id="freeText7220611448221093859" style="display:none">well, at this point I'm beginning to wonder if Nicholas Sparks just writes the books to be made into movies? Just gross. <br />That epilogue really drew me in. It would have been awesome to have a few more of those Stalker perspectives throughout. <br />Also, this one didn't have a ton of cheesy moments, which is great!<br /><br />3 stars <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1804378200" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1804378200" />
    <a title="Allyson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34275651-allyson"><img alt="Allyson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529181856p2/34275651.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1804378200?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allyson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allyson" href="/user/show/34275651-allyson">Allyson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781455520626" href="/book/show/28119197-see-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34275651-allyson?shelf=adult-fiction">adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34275651-allyson?shelf=adult-romance">adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34275651-allyson?shelf=personal-library">personal-library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34275651-allyson?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34275651-allyson?shelf=north-carolina-books">north-carolina-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34275651-allyson?shelf=set-in-the-south">set-in-the-south</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1804378200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6848055973811765236">First things first, it took me an embarrassingly long time to read <i>See Me</i>. This was no fault of the book, but the fact that I soon got distracted with a new Kindle (I own <i>See Me</i> in paperback) kept me from giving the novel the full attention it deserved. Now that I've reached the end, I wish I had finished this book sooner!<br/><br/>Like all Nicholas Sparks novels, <i>See Me</i> takes place in North Carolina, this time in the coastal town of Wilmington. The two main protagonists, Maria and Collin's lives are thro</span>
  <span id="freeText6848055973811765236" style="display:none">First things first, it took me an embarrassingly long time to read <i>See Me</i>. This was no fault of the book, but the fact that I soon got distracted with a new Kindle (I own <i>See Me</i> in paperback) kept me from giving the novel the full attention it deserved. Now that I've reached the end, I wish I had finished this book sooner!<br /><br />Like all Nicholas Sparks novels, <i>See Me</i> takes place in North Carolina, this time in the coastal town of Wilmington. The two main protagonists, Maria and Collin's lives are thrown together when Maria's younger sister, Serena, sets them up. As they begin to develop feelings for one another, Maria's life becomes endangered due to someone's hard feelings from a case she worked on at her previous law firm. Will Maria's life--let alone her budding relationship with Collin--survive the threats of her stalker?<br /><br />To avoid spoilers, I'll now review the highlights of the novel:<br /><br /><u>The Thriller Aspect</u>: Nicholas Sparks is a world-renowned romance novelist, but he's only written a couple other books with thriller aspects (<i>Safe Haven</i> and <i>The Guardian</i>), which are two of my favorites. <i>See Me</i> was as equally well-written in terms of suspense, and the mystery element of identifying Maria's stalker kept me guessing throughout the book. I highly encourage Mr. Sparks to continue to experiment with thriller romances!<br /><u>The Characters</u>: At the beginning, I found Collin hard to relate to, but as his past was revealed, I soon came to love his characterization. Maria is a very relatable protagonist, and I loved her relationship with her sister, Serena. Even the secondary characters had infectious personalities!<br /><u>The Love Story</u>: I loved the way Maria and Collin's relationship transpired. Maria--basically a model citizen--had to come to terms with and accept Collin's rebellious and crime-ridden past. Collin more than redeemed his past mistakes and sacrificed everything in order to protect Maria, which was both adorable and endearing. <br /><u>The Setting</u>: Being a native of eastern NC, I love the setting of Wilmington. I read most of the novel during Hurricane Florence which devastated Wilmington, so it was nice to read about the city in a pleasant light.<br /><br />Overall, I highly enjoyed this novel and am always eager to read more by Mr. Sparks. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6848055973811765236" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1304565933" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1304565933" />
    <a title="Gabby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26560207-gabby"><img alt="Gabby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1482222518p2/26560207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1304565933?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gabby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gabby" href="/user/show/26560207-gabby">Gabby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=disappointed">disappointed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=3-star-books">3-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=lost-interest">lost-interest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=audiobooks-i-listened-to">audiobooks-i-listened-to</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26560207-gabby?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1304565933" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16528422246753084860"><b>2.5 stars</b><br/>I don't really have a lot to say about this book other than it wasn't what I was expecting at all, and not in a good way. I used to love Nicholas Sparks books when I was in high school but recently I've become annoyed with how repetitive and cliche his books are. This book felt 25% romance and 75% thriller, which wasn't necessarily a bad thing, but I couldn't care less about any of the characters. <br/><br/>The romance felt rushed and forced and insta-love like. I related to Maria at times with h</span>
  <span id="freeText16528422246753084860" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars</b><br />I don't really have a lot to say about this book other than it wasn't what I was expecting at all, and not in a good way. I used to love Nicholas Sparks books when I was in high school but recently I've become annoyed with how repetitive and cliche his books are. This book felt 25% romance and 75% thriller, which wasn't necessarily a bad thing, but I couldn't care less about any of the characters. <br /><br />The romance felt rushed and forced and insta-love like. I related to Maria at times with her passion to succeed and her lack of a social life, but other than that she was just an okay female protagonist. Colin's character was likeable at times, but he drove me nuts with his "okay's" as a response to <i>everything</i>, like <b>I GET IT</b>, he's a man of few words, but it gets annoying after a while. I did like the fact that he was more of a "bad boy" and had been in and out of prison which makes him different from Nicholas Sparks typical male love interests. <br /><br />The first half of this book feels like a complete different book from the second half. The first half is a insta-love romance between Maria and Colin, and their romance is completely forgettable by the way, it's nothing special - I'm struggling to remember all their scenes right now. Then the second half of the book becomes this ridiculous thriller with this guy stalking Maria and the sexual harassment going on in Maria's office. I was just really bored and uninterested in the "suspenseful" scenes and I realized I didn't care much for the romance scenes either. <br /><br />One of the scenes I did enjoy though was the first time Colin and Maria meet, when he's helping her fix the tire and his face is all fucked up cause he was in a fight recently, and I just thought it was funny because she was afraid of him. But to be honest that's all I'm really going to remember about this story unfortunately. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16528422246753084860" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3s5YVq2oLVT46gcG9b01RURn9BSYP31jXAyWvdma7x3AcCkTRDn74yZ4iTGboye4MYlVBiSSLTii9AJElujriw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

Pese a las advertencias de otros y sus propias dudas, soportó mares tempestuosos, cientos de horas en el agua, medusas venenosas y muchos otros peligros para alcanzar su sueño.Pero ningún logro es un incidente aislado y ésta no es la excepción. Por eso, Travesía interminable no sólo relata las apasionantes aventuras de Antonio en el agua; también cuenta la historia de un niño hiperactivo y con sobrepeso que descubriría la natación, perseguiría un sueño olímpico, asistiría a la Universidad de Stanford y, más tarde, se adentraría en el mundo enredoso de la política mexicana. En el camino llevaría Speedo a México, organizaría los primeros triatlones en su país y viviría en carne propia las secuelas de un infame asesinato político. Ésta es una historia de riesgo, temor, confianza, fracasos y pérdidas; muestra cómo la capacidad de adaptarse, concentrar esfuerzos y controlar la mente permitió a Antonio superar cada revés que buscaba derribarlo dentro y fuera del dramatic ways this relationship complicates and enriches their lives, and the lives of the people they love.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"17876744184543925598\" href=\"#\"       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks">About Nicholas Sparks</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/2345.Nicholas_Sparks"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1591799426p3/2345.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9490198165781234428">Nicholas Sparks is one of the world’s most beloved storytellers. All of his books have been <i>New York Times</i> bestsellers, with over 105 million copies sold worldwide, in more than 50 languages, including over 75 million copies in the United States alone.<br/><br/>Sparks wrote one of his best-known stories, <i>The Notebook</i>, over a period of six months at age 28. It was published in 1996 and he followed with the n</span>
  <span id="freeText9490198165781234428" style="display:none">Nicholas Sparks is one of the world’s most beloved storytellers. All of his books have been <i>New York Times</i> bestsellers, with over 105 million copies sold worldwide, in more than 50 languages, including over 75 million copies in the United States alone.<br /><br />Sparks wrote one of his best-known stories, <i>The Notebook</i>, over a period of six months at age 28. It was published in 1996 and he followed with the novels <i>Message in a Bottle</i> (1998), <i>A Walk to Remember</i> (1999), <i>The Rescue</i> (2000), <i>A Bend in the Road</i> (2001), <i>Nights in Rodanthe</i> (2002), <i>The Guardian</i> (2003), <i>The Wedding</i> (2003), <i>True Believer</i> (2005) and its sequel, <i>At First Sight</i> (2005), <i>Dear John</i> (2006), <i>The Choice</i> (2007), <i>The Lucky One</i> (2008), <i>The Last Song</i> (2009), <i>Safe Haven</i> (2010), <i>The Best of Me</i> (2011), <i>The Longest Ride</i> (2013), <i>See Me</i> (2015), <i>Two by Two</i> (2016) and Every Breath (2018) as well as the 2004 non-fiction memoir <i>Three Weeks With My Brother</i>, co-written with his brother Micah. His twenty-first novel, <i>The Return</i>, will be published on September 29, 2020.<br /><br />Film adaptations of Nicholas Sparks novels, including <i>The Choice</i>, <i>The Longest Ride</i>, <i>The Best of Me</i>, <i>Safe Haven</i> (on all of which he served as a producer), <i>The Lucky One</i>, <i>Message in a Bottle</i>, <i>A Walk to Remember</i>,<i> The Notebook</i>, <i>Nights in Rodanthe</i>, <i>Dear John</i> and <i>The Last Song</i>, have had a cumulative worldwide gross of over three-quarters of a billion dollars. <i> The Notebook</i> is also being adapted into a musical, featuring music and lyrics by Ingrid Michaelson. <br /><br />Sparks lives in North Carolina. He contributes to a variety of local and national charities, and is a major contributor to the Creative Writing Program (MFA) at the University of Notre Dame, where he provides scholarships, internships, and a fellowship annually. He co-founded The Epiphany School in New Bern, North Carolina in 2006. As a former full scholarship athlete (he still holds a track and field record at the University of Notre Dame) he also spent four years coaching track and field athletes at the local public high school. In 2009, the team he coached at New Bern High School set a World Junior Indoor Record in the 4x400 meter, in New York. The record still stands. <br /><br />The Nicholas Sparks Foundation, a 501(c)(3) nonprofit committed to improving cultural and international understanding through global education experiences for students of all ages was launched in 2011. Between the foundation, and the personal gifts of the Sparks family, more than $15 million dollars have been distributed to deserving charities, scholarship programs, and projects. Because the Sparks family covers all operational expenses of the foundation, 100% of donations are devoted to programs.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9490198165781234428" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
